$(document).ready(function() {
    var autoCompleteJsMenuSearch = new autoComplete({
        selector: "#menuQuickSearch_menuQuickSearch",
        data: {
            src: menus,
            keys: ['menuTitle', 'combinedMenuTitle'],
            filter: function(list) {
              var uniqueListItems = [];
              var matched = [];
              list.forEach(function(listItem) {
                  if (matched.indexOf(listItem.value.id) === -1) {
                      matched.push(listItem.value.id);
                      uniqueListItems.push(listItem);
                  }
              })
              return uniqueListItems;
            }
        },
        resultsList: {
            id: "menuQuickSearchResultList",
            maxResults: 500,
        },
        resultItem: {
            element: function(item, data) {
                $(item).html('');
                var menuData = data.value;
                var combinedMenuTitle = menuData.combinedMenuTitle;
                combinedMenuTitle = combinedMenuTitle.substring(combinedMenuTitle.indexOf("&gt;") + 1, combinedMenuTitle.lastIndexOf("&gt;")).trim();
                combinedMenuTitle = $('&lt;div/&gt;').addClass('combined-menu-title').text(combinedMenuTitle);
                var menuTitle = $('&lt;div/&gt;').addClass('menu-title').text(menuData.menuTitle);
                $(item).append(menuTitle);
                $(item).append(combinedMenuTitle);
            },
            selected: "menuSearchSelected",
            class: "menuSearchResultItem",
        },
     });
    document.querySelector("#menuQuickSearch_menuQuickSearch").addEventListener("selection", function(event) {
        //this content is overridden from previewAppraisalQuestionFormSuccess.js and defaultViewSuccess.js files. make sure to change those if any changes are done.
        var item = event.detail.selection.value;
        if (item.linkAttributes.target &amp;&amp; item.linkAttributes.target == '_blank') {
            sessionStorage.removeItem('current_menu');
            window.top.open(item.linkAttributes.href,'_blank');
        } else if (item.api_request_url) {
            window.top.location = item.api_request_url;
        } else {
            window.top.location = item.linkAttributes.href;
        }
        $("#menuQuickSearch_menuQuickSearch").val('');
    });
    
    document.querySelector("#menuQuickSearch_menuQuickSearch").addEventListener("close", function() {
        $("#menuQuickSearch_menuQuickSearch").blur();
    });
 });
 </script>

            <script>
    sessionStorage.current_menu = '';
    sessionStorage.current_menu_id = '';
    var homePageURL = '/client/#/dashboard';
    $(document).ready(function() {
        jQuery('#logoutLink').click(function() {
            scheduleNavigationLog();
        });
    });

    function scheduleNavigationLog() {
        var navigationLog = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("navigation_log"));//NOSONAR
        if (!navigationLog || navigationLog.length == 0) {
            navigationLog = [];
        }
        var currentTime = (new Date()).toISOString().slice(0, 19).replace('T', ' ');
        var latestLog = sessionStorage.getItem("navigation_log_latest");
        if (!latestLog) {
            latestLog = localStorage.getItem("navigation_log_latest");//NOSONAR
        }
        latestLog = JSON.parse(latestLog);
        navigationLog.push({from: latestLog.to, to: '/auth/login', time: currentTime});

        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (24*60*60*1000));
        expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
        document.cookie = "navigation_log" + "=" + JSON.stringify(navigationLog) + expires + "; path=/";
        localStorage.setItem("navigation_log", JSON.stringify([]));//NOSONAR
        localStorage.setItem("navigation_logged_time", new Date());//NOSONAR
    }

    $('#homeIndicator').click(function (event) {
        event.preventDefault();
        var newHref = window.location.origin + homePageURL;
        if (newHref == window.location.href) {
            window.location.reload();
        } else {
            window.location.replace(homePageURL);
        }
    });


    jQuery('#displayAbout').click(function(event) {
        event.stopImmediatePropagation();
    });

    $(document).on('click', '.top-level-menu-item, .sub-menu-item-link, .menu-level-2 &gt; a', function () {
        setClickedOnForNavigationTracking('main_menu')
    });

    function setClickedOnForNavigationTracking(source) {
        localStorage.setItem('clickedOn',source)
    }

    window.handleKeyPress = function(e,source){
        var key = e.which;
        if(key == 13){
            setClickedOnForNavigationTracking(source);
        }
    };

    $(document).on('click', '#sidebar-profile-picture .image-container .password-action', function () {
        $('#sidebar-profile-picture .sub-menu-container-php').toggleClass('opened');
    });
    $(document).on('click', '#sidebar-profile-picture .sub-menu-container-php .sub-menu-item-link', function () {
        $('#sidebar-profile-picture .sub-menu-container-php').removeClass('opened');
    });
    $(document).on('click', function (event) {
        if ($(event.target).closest('.profile-context-menu-handler').length == 0 &amp;&amp; !$(event.target).hasClass('profile-context-menu-handler')) {
            $('#sidebar-profile-picture .sub-menu-container-php').removeClass('opened');
        }
    });
    $(document).on('click', '#aboutDisplayLink', function (event) {
        event.preventDefault();
        $('body').append($('#displayAbout'));
        $('#displayAbout').openModal({
            ready: function(modal, trigger) {
                var loadMask = $('#displayAboutLoadMask');
                if (loadMask.length &gt; 0) {
                    $.get('/communication/beaconAbout', function(data) {
                        $('#displayAbout div.modal-content').html(data);
                    })
                }
            }
        });
        $('#displayAbout').css('z-index', 1012);
        $('body &gt; div.lean-overlay').css('z-index', 1011);
    });

    $(document).on('click', '#sidebar-toggle', function(e) {
        document.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("collapsibleViewToggled", { bubbles: true }));
        if ($('#left-menu').hasClass('menu-visible')) {
            $('#left-menu, #right-side, #right-side &gt; header').addClass('menu-hidden').removeClass('menu-visible');
            $('.main-menu-item-1').addClass('hidden');
            $('.main-menu-item-2').removeClass('hidden');
        } else {
            $('#left-menu, #right-side, #right-side &gt; header').addClass('menu-visible').removeClass('menu-hidden');
            $('.main-menu-item-1').removeClass('hidden');
            $('.main-menu-item-2').addClass('hidden');
        }
    });

    (function() {
        var timeout;

        var menu = document.getElementById('menu-container');
        menu.addEventListener('scroll', showHideSideMenuMoreLink);
        window.addEventListener('resize', showHideSideMenuMoreLink);
        document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').addEventListener('click', showHideSideMenuMoreLink);

        function showHideSideMenuMoreLink() {

            if (timeout) {
                clearTimeout(timeout);
            }

            timeout = setTimeout(function() {
                var showMoreLink = false;

                /* Show more link if element is overflowing vertically and is not scrolled to the bottom */
                var overflowAmount = menu.scrollHeight - menu.clientHeight;

                var amountScrolledDown = menu.scrollHeight - Math.abs(menu.scrollTop);// === element.clientHeight
                console.log('overflowAmount=' + overflowAmount + ', amountScrolledDown = ' + amountScrolledDown +
                    ', clientHeight = ' + menu.clientHeight);

                if (overflowAmount &gt; 20 &amp;&amp; Math.abs(amountScrolledDown - menu.clientHeight) &gt; 20) {
                    showMoreLink = true;
                }
                var moreLink = document.getElementById('side-menu-more');
                moreLink.style.display = showMoreLink ? 'flex' : 'none';
            }, 200);
        }

        showHideSideMenuMoreLink();

        var moreLink = document.getElementById('side-menu-more');
        moreLink.addEventListener('click', function (event) {

            event.preventDefault();

            // Log the clicked element in the console
            if (!menu.scrollBy) {
                menu.scrollTop += 100;
            } else {
                menu.scrollBy({top: 100, left: 0, behavior: 'smooth'});
            }

        }, false);
    })();

</script>
